<span id="freeTextContainer15707952060140876753">Lara Cameron is a famous powerful wealthy New York building developer who struggled from brutal poverty in Glace Bay, a banker who took her body as part of her first deal, to Chicago, banker Keller whose love she takes lightly for granted. As her skyscrapers and boutique hotels tower on earth, she is at the top of a male dominated field. She lies and cheats to close a deal</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText15707952060140876753">Lara Cameron is a famous powerful wealthy New York building developer who struggled from brutal poverty in Glace Bay, a banker who took her body as part of her first deal, to Chicago, banker Keller whose love she takes lightly for granted. As her skyscrapers and boutique hotels tower on earth, she is at the top of a male dominated field. She lies and cheats to close a deal, making cruel enemies. She is forty, beautiful, glamorous, insecure, ruthless, vulnerable, secretly generous, rich - and still wants more. She marries an international concert pianist, the Lochinvar of her childhood dreams, but aomeone puts him in the hospital and threatens to take down her empire.</span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_162031822">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/162031822" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/4218875-kwesi" class="left imgcol" title="Kwesi ???"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1402930457p2/4218875.jpg" alt="Kwesi ???" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/162031822?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">May 10, 2011</a>

      <a href="/user/show/4218875-kwesi" class="user" title="Kwesi ???">Kwesi ???</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it">really liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/1795294.The_Stars_Shine_Down" title="Hardcover 9780688084905" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/4218875-kwesi?shelf=owned" class="actionLinkLite">owned</a>, 
              <a href="/review/list/4218875-kwesi?shelf=2011" class="actionLinkLite">2011</a>, 
              <a href="/review/list/4218875-kwesi?shelf=sidney-sheldon" class="actionLinkLite">sidney-sheldon</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer162031822">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9749717474499418584">I promised myself not to write a review, but GR is so tempting. I'm currently sitting, waiting, waiting for the right time to stand. Imagining the high buildings, the towers and even the tallest skyscraper built in Dubai. <em>I can't pronounce the word skyscraper, boo.</em> A skyscraper is a tall, habitable building, no definite height as long as it gets higher and higher.<br /><br />One of the most iconic and popular skyscraper built in New York was the <em>World Trade Center</em>. Built on 1973 and stood for 23 years after</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText9749717474499418584">I promised myself not to write a review, but GR is so tempting. I'm currently sitting, waiting, waiting for the right time to stand. Imagining the high buildings, the towers and even the tallest skyscraper built in Dubai. <em>I can't pronounce the word skyscraper, boo.</em> A skyscraper is a tall, habitable building, no definite height as long as it gets higher and higher.<br /><br />One of the most iconic and popular skyscraper built in New York was the <em>World Trade Center</em>. Built on 1973 and stood for 23 years after the great suicide attack forcing it to collide in full height causing thousands of deaths and millions of mourners to pray for the soul and the survivors. It was one of the worst terrorist attack happened, when the news flashed a picture of <em>Bin Laden</em> informing the casualties that he died when American armies entered his territory last week my cousin said that she can't forget the days that the people mourned for the 3,000 deaths including Filipinos and some foreigners.<br /><br />On September 24, 2004, the tallest skyscraper was beginning to rise through the wide sky and in 2009 it was finished with great satisfaction and named as the tallest man-made skyscraper. The <em>Burj Dubai</em> designed by <em>Adrian Smith</em> and his team creating a marvelous, luxurious habitable building defeating the tallest pyramid in Asia, <em>Great Pyramid of Giza</em>. <em>I'm not interested to buy a room in that building, remember the earthquakes.</em> In 1992, Sidney Sheldon wrote his first attempt to build a skyscraper by his well-know protagonist, <strong>Lara Cameron</strong>, by writing an interesting yet claimable masterpiece as she journey through man's world, real estate.<br /><br /><strong>Lara Cameron</strong>, born in Nova Scotia, her mother died in childbirth with her twin and her hopeless dad took care of her, or maybe not. She was never given any attention, no money to buy new clothes, to own things, to go to school, and secluded from other children. When her father died, she realized she have to face the future, the strength that she needed must be zipped off from her so she face her greatest challenge, to dominate man's world, real estate.<br /><br />As she venture through years, meeting people, enemies and friends, losing them one by one, building skyscrapers, parks, condominiums and etc. She achieved far from what she imagined, a strong willed woman who wants to be the empress of her own kingdom as she built her structures higher and higher. But when a tragedy happened to her husband, she soon been accused causing herself to carry the weights. Can she survive in the end or another destiny that the Faiths destined to her to suffer like her father?<br /><br />A very interesting and commercially written for everyone to enjoyed, not only for female but to everyone who really interested in reading a fast-paced and informative book. The beginning until the end, the book was so boring keeping you to continue reading but the near end was so shockingly interesting. Sidney Sheldon cannot missed such great writing style, pulling the readers till the end and giving twisted lines. A must read!<br /><br /><a rel="nofollow" href="http://oldfashionedreader.blogspot.com/2011/05/stars-shine-down-by-sidney-sheldon.html">
  <img class="escapedImg" src="http://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380348592i/702824._SX540_.jpg" /></a><br /><blockquote>A <a rel="nofollow" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hymenocallis">Hymenocallis</a> flower showing six spokes, as pattern for the three-lobed design - <a rel="nofollow" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Burj_Khalifa">Wikipedia</a>
</blockquote><br /><br /><strong>Rating</strong> - <em>The Stars Shine Down</em> by Sidney Sheldon, <strong>4 Sweets</strong> and concrete jungle where dreams are made! (So far, I was impressed by how Sidney Sheldon wrote this book, although he doesn't have any idea and experience in playing the real estate. Kudos, and in the end friendship and love will always conquer everything. Spoiler! But still, I highly recommend his <em>Master of the Game</em>)<br /><br /><strong>Challenges</strong>:<br /><em>Book #72 for 2011</em><br /><em>Book #44 for <a rel="nofollow" href="http://bareadingchallenges.blogspot.com/p/off-shelf-challenge.html">Off the Shelf!</a><br /><br /><a rel="nofollow" href="http://oldfashionedreader.blogspot.com/2011/05/stars-shine-down-by-sidney-sheldon.html"><img class="escapedImg" src="http://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380341493i/697602.jpg" /></a></em></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/458980654?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Jan 15, 2015</a>

      <a href="/user/show/4863716-an-odd1" class="user" title="An Odd1">An Odd1</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="did not like it">did not like it</span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="did not like it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="did not like it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="did not like it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="did not like it"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer458980654">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6696769806108519399">Stunningly beautiful Lara Cameron on her fortieth birthday, having just lost her fame and fortune as foremost (only female) building developer in Chicago, then New York, her name plastered on the highest deluxe hotels and offices, reviews her life. Born unwanted to an impoverished drunk in Glace Bay, she takes over his rent collection when he is dying. Her first banker, ugly and fat, makes her first deal dependent on having her virgin body. I almost gave up reading. <br /><br />Her Chicago banker Howard Kel</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText6696769806108519399">Stunningly beautiful Lara Cameron on her fortieth birthday, having just lost her fame and fortune as foremost (only female) building developer in Chicago, then New York, her name plastered on the highest deluxe hotels and offices, reviews her life. Born unwanted to an impoverished drunk in Glace Bay, she takes over his rent collection when he is dying. Her first banker, ugly and fat, makes her first deal dependent on having her virgin body. I almost gave up reading. <br /><br />Her Chicago banker Howard Keller falls in love, but she treats him as an employee. She privately helps employees with health problems, but lies and connives to get deals done, making a bad enemy of competing developer Steve Murchison. <br /><br />Union trouble leads to a long-time lover, Mafia lawyer Paul Martin 65. Apparently Sicilian Mafia began to combat corrupt government, so Ivo Martino, ten when a powerful land owner had local police torture his father, chop off his privates, stuff them in his mouth, and kill his mother too. Years later, grown powerful himself, the boy performed the same punishment on the landlord, then fled with his family to America. Was this Paul's life? No, his grandfather's. Did author research flash dollar signs so the incident had to be included? I almost quit again.<br /><br />International famous pianist Philip Adler is the living picture of Lara's childhood imaginary Lochinvar, so despite nothing in common, she wants him for a husband. I foresee trouble with Paul, and am tired of her pate and champagne, private jets and hoity toity lifestyle. I skip to the end, then check back a bit. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span style="display: none" class="spoilerContainer">[<br /><br />Philip hospitalized after an attack, Lara blames Paul. But testifying in court, rejected Paul protects her. Jealous Howard is the mastermind villain that tried to take her down. In the car with recovered Philip, she sees a potential site, and we realize she is still ambitious and hasn't learned anything. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I could have quit at the beginning.<!--["br"]--><!--["br"]--><!--["br"]--><!--["br"]--><!--["br"]--><!--["br"]--><!--["br"]--><!--["br"]--></span>

      <a href="/user/show/10702720-alchris-m" class="user" title="Alchris M.">Alchris M.</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing">it was amazing</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/84054.The_Stars_Shine_Down" title="Paperback 9780006178712" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer374908670">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7881765499435984251">The Stars Shine Down is the story of Lara Cameron, a self-made billionaire who had dominated the world of real estate—which, according to the book, is mostly dominated by men, as portrayed in other characters used in the story. My opinions on different aspects of the story vary as follows:<br /><br />1.) The story of Lara being from rags to riches sounds a little impossible, more like a fairy-tale-type of story. But it's Sidney's story, so I give him that right to tell his story and develop characters any w</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText7881765499435984251">The Stars Shine Down is the story of Lara Cameron, a self-made billionaire who had dominated the world of real estate—which, according to the book, is mostly dominated by men, as portrayed in other characters used in the story. My opinions on different aspects of the story vary as follows:<br /><br />1.) The story of Lara being from rags to riches sounds a little impossible, more like a fairy-tale-type of story. But it's Sidney's story, so I give him that right to tell his story and develop characters any way he wanted to.<br /><br />2.) In this story, Sidney had proven himself once again as a "Wizard of Words." As a writer myself, I admire authors who can actually write detailed sex scenes without being too vulgar. Sheldon did that with his metaphor with the act of having sex to the storm and the buildings, as well as the curtains and ripples and shadows. 100 stars for that!<br /><br />3.) Relating the title to some scenes in the story somehow—as silly as it may sound—gave me tears. This is the only book that had done that to me, Sheldon being the only author. "The stars shine down and watch us live our little lives and weep for us..."<br /><br />4.) Some twists in the story were like fallacies. But that's an element in thriller and suspense writing, innit?<br /><br />4.) The ending somehow didn't leave a lasting impression to me. Or perhaps, I've expected something similar to Sidney's "The Other Side Of Midnight." It's good though that Sidney made this one less tragic.<br /><br />I'd still give Sheldon 5 stars for this novel. He's a wizard of words. I like his prose. Fantastic author. He's the only author whose genre I despise yet can still entice me to read up to the very last page.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="7881765499435984251">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <a href="/user/show/11737688-serene-wong" class="user" title="Serene Wong">Serene Wong</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing">it was amazing</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer739031914">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2410387096560651219">THIS BOOK ROCKS. I can't think of any good words to say about this book actually - it is indescribable.<br /><br />Okay, I shall go on to explain why.<br /><br />Lara Cameron is born with a jack-ass of a father who refuses to acknowledge her in his life, calling her a "jinx" creating all sorts of problems for her. What made matters worse is that her mother had died giving birth to her, which added to all the tension. As a result, Lara grew up without a mother's love AND a father's love, being outcast by the students in</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText2410387096560651219">THIS BOOK ROCKS. I can't think of any good words to say about this book actually - it is indescribable.<br /><br />Okay, I shall go on to explain why.<br /><br />Lara Cameron is born with a jack-ass of a father who refuses to acknowledge her in his life, calling her a "jinx" creating all sorts of problems for her. What made matters worse is that her mother had died giving birth to her, which added to all the tension. As a result, Lara grew up without a mother's love AND a father's love, being outcast by the students in her school who liked to bully her upon knowing she does not have any parents. Her father works at a boarding house in which he needs to collect rents from the tenants and return to the landlord at the end of the month. The boarding house is where Lara starts to become more independent - while her father nearly died (unfortunately in a bad way) resting in a hospital, Lara was the one who went around to help collect dues owed and replaced her father's position. This impressed the landlord however, he was a bastard who intend to take advantage of Lara.<br />Fast forward, Lara became an impressive owner of hotels and she managed to make her mark in a man's dominated field - real estate. The put downs and humiliation by the men she had come across had not stopped her determination to succeed. What is inspiring about this novel is that a woman's inner strength is so strong that others can't help but stop to admire and respect her.<br /><br />I feel that Lara has many good and strong points. Firstly, though she has a stoic stone cold woman facade, beneath all that lies a gold heart. This is evident in how she treats her employees as though they are her family - a family she could never have, properly.<br /><br />I am glad she finally found her happily ever after with the pianist.<br /><br />The Stars Shine Down truly deserve an accolade.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="2410387096560651219">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1261562013">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer51745189251628940">One of the reasons why I like Shidney Sheldon's books is because he usually has strong women protagonist and this book did too. The book is about a successful real estate businesswomen Lara. The book begins with an epilogue where Lara is going to celebrate her 40th birthday in the highest building of the United States, built by her. The story portrays Lara as a firm, nononsense ambitious woman who does "anything" to get her job done. Like the usual Shidney Sheldon stories, the protagonist faces</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText51745189251628940">One of the reasons why I like Shidney Sheldon's books is because he usually has strong women protagonist and this book did too. The book is about a successful real estate businesswomen Lara. The book begins with an epilogue where Lara is going to celebrate her 40th birthday in the highest building of the United States, built by her. The story portrays Lara as a firm, nononsense ambitious woman who does "anything" to get her job done. Like the usual Shidney Sheldon stories, the protagonist faces difficult situations, connects with the Mafia, becomes ridiculously rich, makes friends and enemies too. I liked how the author portrayed the background story of prime characters and described Lara's success vividly.Compared to other books, by Sheldon, this was an average one. There were no surprising elements- the stories were kind of predictable. I liked the ending of the story. Overall, a nice, light book to read.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11469185410525291907">Dreadful. Simply dreadful. While I can admit to taking pleasure from some of Sheldon's frothy soap style novels, this one takes the genre to new lows.<br /><br />It's the usual beautiful woman who claws her way to the top amongst intrigue and sexual discrimination. There's the love interest, also heavily endowed with wealth and talent (of course...)and the disasters and calamities that befall them as they try valiantly to stay together.<br /><br />It's paint by numbers, at best...</span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_909980839">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/909980839" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/8345408-leanne-hunt" class="left imgcol" title="Leanne Hunt"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1335095657p2/8345408.jpg" alt="Leanne Hunt" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/909980839?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Apr 28, 2014</a>

      <a href="/user/show/8345408-leanne-hunt" class="user" title="Leanne Hunt">Leanne Hunt</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it">really liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/84054.The_Stars_Shine_Down" title="Paperback 9780006178712" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/8345408-leanne-hunt?shelf=women-in-business" class="actionLinkLite">women-in-business</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer909980839">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17414320793738728966">For an insight into property development, this novel is great. I read it years ago and always remembered it as the book that inspired me with regard to buying, building and renovating spaces for living in. It is a story of courage, success, struggle and survival which leaves the reader feeling motivated to be part of the refurbishment of cities.<br /><br />As light entertainment, Lara Cameron's story of rags to riches moves quickly and incorporates family drama, intrigue, romance and suspense. Sidney Sheldo</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText17414320793738728966">For an insight into property development, this novel is great. I read it years ago and always remembered it as the book that inspired me with regard to buying, building and renovating spaces for living in. It is a story of courage, success, struggle and survival which leaves the reader feeling motivated to be part of the refurbishment of cities.<br /><br />As light entertainment, Lara Cameron's story of rags to riches moves quickly and incorporates family drama, intrigue, romance and suspense. Sidney Sheldon is a master at capturing the essence of story, providing a plot that is well-formed and satisfying. However, character exploration is not of much interest to him and the reader who is accustomed to rich, complex characters should put aside this expectation in order to enjoy what this book has to offer. To me, his style is closer to that of a movie script than a work of fiction, which is understandable because he worked for so many years as a successful screenwriter. Incidentally, his autobiography, "The Other Side Of Me" is well worth a read.<br /><br />As I indicated at the start of this review, what I appreciated most about this book was its setting and content. The real estate boom in the seventies and eighties provides the perfect background for Lara Cameron's meteoric rise to fame and power, and the kinds of challenges she faces on a daily basis reflect the nature of the industry. Her long-term partnership with one-time baseball star Howard Keller, her affair with Mafia-linked Paul Martin and her romance with concert pianist Philip Adler all add variety and spice to the story. In the end, although the characters are minimally sketched and the business situations simply portrayed, the message itself is compelling; namely, that a woman with vision and courage can make a lasting difference, if not on the skyline of a city then most certainly in her intimate relationships.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="17414320793738728966">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it">liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span></span>

              <a href="/review/list/3841473-kate-s?shelf=2013" class="actionLinkLite">2013</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer721534750">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2738932134350840097">Sidney Sheldon's books are such a guilty pleasure for me. I like the conniving characters and the variety of situations which are set up for his protagonists to overcome and even the crazy coincidences which mean success for the good guys. This was no exception, but there was nothing really new in this story and I did not like Lara as much as I liked Kate from <a title="Master of the Game by Sidney Sheldon" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/43330.Master_of_the_Game">Master of the Game</a> or Tracey from <a title="If Tomorrow Comes by Sidney Sheldon" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14554.If_Tomorrow_Comes">If Tomorrow Comes</a>, but still I enjoyed it enough.</span>

          </span>

  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1432089061" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/3515571-meta-morfillah" class="left imgcol" title="Meta Morfillah"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1269961098p2/3515571.jpg" alt="Meta Morfillah" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/1432089061?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Nov 02, 2015</a>

      <a href="/user/show/3515571-meta-morfillah" class="user" title="Meta Morfillah">Meta Morfillah</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing">it was amazing</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/2116783.The_Stars_Shine_Down" title="Paperback 979605549X" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1432089061">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5080379922747491585">Judul: Kilau bintang menerangi bumi<br />Penulis: Sidney sheldon<br />Penerbit: Gramedia Pustaka Utama Jakarta<br />Dimensi: Tahun 2003, 319 hlm, ebook, no ISBN<br /><br />Kisah diawali dengan perayaan ulang tahun Lara di Grand Ballroom Cameron Plaza miliknya. Dengan 200 undangan orang-orang penting dan berpengaruh yang menjadi tamunya, di tengah buruknya publisitas mengenai dirinya dan kerajaan real estate yang dirintisnya. Dalam perjalanan menuju lokasi itu, cerita bergulir perlahan menggunakan alur mundur, begitu seterusn</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText5080379922747491585">Judul: Kilau bintang menerangi bumi<br />Penulis: Sidney sheldon<br />Penerbit: Gramedia Pustaka Utama Jakarta<br />Dimensi: Tahun 2003, 319 hlm, ebook, no ISBN<br /><br />Kisah diawali dengan perayaan ulang tahun Lara di Grand Ballroom Cameron Plaza miliknya. Dengan 200 undangan orang-orang penting dan berpengaruh yang menjadi tamunya, di tengah buruknya publisitas mengenai dirinya dan kerajaan real estate yang dirintisnya. Dalam perjalanan menuju lokasi itu, cerita bergulir perlahan menggunakan alur mundur, begitu seterusnya, semakin mundur hingga ke masa kanak-kanaknya dan menjelaskan gaya khas penulis dalam menegaskan karakter tokoh dan motifnya. Pun hal yang sama terjadi pada karakter tokoh penjelas lainnya. Tokoh utama kita kali ini, Lara Cameron, diceritakan sebagai pengusaha real estate yang mengesankan dan berhasil dalam bidang yang didominasi pria, hingga mendapat julukan "kupu-kupu besi". Hal itu didapatkannya dari tempaan hidup yang keras, di mana penderitaan akan kemiskinan dan cinta ia hadapi. Ayah yang tak mencintainya, lingkungan yang memaksanya cepat dewasa dalam usia sedemikian muda serta rendahnya penilaian orang akan kecerdasan dirinya, semata hanya melihat keindahan tubuhnya.<br /><br />Hidupnya mulai berubah sebab ia adalah orang yang peka pada kebutuhan orang lain. Salah satu tamu istimewa, Charles Cohn, membantunya melihat dunia dan mendukung ke arah yang baik. Meski proses pertama bangunan yang ia rintis harus dibayar dengan keperawanannya, Lara bertekad ia akan terus menghiasi kota yang ia incar dengan bangunan miliknya. Tekad itu semakin kuat dan nyata, disertai keberanian mengambil risiko dan berjudi dengan segala kemungkinan. Perlahan ia menemukan orang yang bisa ia percaya. Howard Keller, mantan bintang olahraga bisbol yang merelakan mimpinya demi merawat ibu tercinta dan beralih menjadi bankir, yang juga memendam rasa cinta pada Lara. Lalu ada Paul Martin, pengacara sekaligus Mafia Sisilia yang mencintai Lara dan cemburu saat tahu Lara menikah dengan orang lain. Philip Adler, pianis berbakat yang berhasil membuatnya melabuhkan hati.<br /><br />Alur cerita terus bergerak mendeskripsikan beragam masalah dan keputusan yang diambil Lara dalam membangun kerajaannya. Juga beragam isu yang terjadi saat Lara sibuk berpikir tentang mewujudkan impiannya. Konflik yang hadir berulang kali adalah beragam negosiasi yang hampir batal, kalah tender, dan beragam hambatan dalam pembangunan gedung yang direncanakan. Namun konflik utama dan menjadi ending dalam kisah ini, adalah kasus penyerangan terhadap Philips, suami Lara dan tuduhan kecurangan dalam pembangunan kasini di Reno yang terkait Paul Martin. Semua bermuara pada cinta. Kecemburuan, kekecewaan, dan harapan memiliki Lara. Semua itu bersetting di beberapa kota seperti Skotlandia, Nova Scotia, Chicago, New York, London, Roma, dan Reno.<br /><br />Awalnya, saya bingung menangkap kaitan judul novel ini dengan isi cerita. Meskipun ada sedikit kutipan di awal novel ini yang berbunyi<br /><br />"Bintang berkilau menerangi bumi<br />Dan menyaksikan kita<br />Menjalani hidup kita yang remeh<br />Dan menangis buat kita" Moneft nodlehs<br /><br />Saya kira semacam perumpamaan Tuhan atau takdir. Tapi di isi cerita, pada perjumpaan pertama Lara dengan Philip, Philip yang diibaratkan bagai kilau bintang menerangi bumi. Dan memang hanya ialah harta yang dimiliki Lara.<br /><br />Beragam tips saat negosiasi dengan latar kultur berbeda dan psikologi manusia pun ada di novel ini, contohnya pada halaman 8 saat Lara memanfaatkan momen jetlag bankir Jepang untuk meeting dan memenangkan semua keputusan. Begitu juga psikologi warna saat membungkus kado bagi orang Jepang.<br /><br />Jika ada tokoh Villain, yang diciptakan sebagai antagonis namun membuat pembaca iba dan merasa dia adalah protagonis, dalam novel ini saya jatuh iba pada Howard Keller. Begitu pun Lara Cameron.<br /><br />Tak perlu diragukan, gaya bahasa penulis memikat seperti biasanya. Membuat saya betah membacanya seharian dan tak ingin beranjak hingga selesai. Seperti biasanya pula, penulis tidak pernah membiarkan semuanya terjadi sesuai dengan tebakan pembaca. Dia selalu berhasil dengan twist dan ending yang tak terduga dan tentu saja: happy ending!<br /><br />Ini adalah novel kelima sidney yang saya baca. Sejujurnya, konflik dalam novel ini tidak begitu berat dibanding empat novel lainnya. Tapi, menarik... bahkan membumi sekali dengan tokohnya yang menurut saya manusiawi dan semacam roman. Terutama tokoh Lara yang merupakan paradoks. Mengalami masa kecil yang tidak bahagia, berusaha merebut kasih sayang ayahnya namun tak diakui, tapi tetap menghargai masa lalunya dengan menatap dan membicarakan yang indah meski tak ingin kembali lagi terhubung dengan masa lalu tersebut. Ia tidak dendam pada masa lalunya yang menjadikannya seperti sekarang ini. Memotivasi saya untuk tetap berpikiran positif, sederhana dan berbaik sangka. Yakin bahwa tetap masih banyak orang baik yang ada di dunia ini.<br /><br />Saya apresiasi 5 dari 5 bintang.<br /><br />"Aku begitu bahagia sehingga aku takut. Aku takut kalau satu pagi aku bangun dan mendapati ternyata semua ini hanya mimpi. Aku tidak pernah menyangka tadinya bahwa orang bisa merasa begini bahagia." (Hlm. 234)<br /><br />"Hati-hati dengan apa yang kauinginkan, karena itu benar-benar bisa terjadi atas dirimu." (Hlm. 270)<br /><br />Meta morfillah</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="5080379922747491585">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span style="display:none" id="freeText9664843387814092784">THE STARS SHINE DOWN<br />Author: Sidney Sheldon <br />Status: World bestseller<br />Year Read: 2015<br />Interest level: 4.5 out of 5.0<br /><br />Star Rating: 4.4<br /><br />Synopsis: there she was, the daughter of a drunk and a mean man who would have nothing to do with hee, and through sheet determination and will, she moved up the ladder and from Glace Bay to Chicago to New York, she became the very best real estate developer of the international level. But she has enemies along the way, and the one man who was her chief backer to be her chief protector and also her near-nemesis.... will she win, or lose? <br /><br />This book is like all the other Sheldon novels: if deals with a poor bitch who rose through the ranks to become one of the very best there is in the male dominated world she's ensconced in. However, as much as it is very interesting, I have to say that Sheldon had become very formulaic In the sense that he uses the very same techniques for writing all fields of his books. His ingenuity is not to be faulted, but why always talk about the same 'she's one of the richest women of the world' stuff. It seriously gets boring after the first ten books or thereabouts. Why!!? New things are made to be filled in the works, not going over the same storyline over and over again incessantly using different characters and backgrounds. <br /><br /><br />Thankfully, my affairs with Sidney Sheldon is at an end because i have finally managed, with this book, to finish the very last novel written by the master storyteller. But to be frank, this book, though beautifully written, is old because the author overflogs the issue of rich whatever whatever..<br /><br />Thank you for reading this, and expect moi to give you more.. <br /><br />You can hit up my blog for other reviews: <a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.kingsleyadrian.wordpress.com" target="_blank">www.kingsleyadrian.wordpress.com</a> <br /><br />Oops, lest I forget, here is the link to my new erotic novella, and I hope you enjoy it, Love The Angel :<br /><a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/dp/ASIN/B00ZIY03HS" target="_blank">http://www.amazon.com/dp/ASIN/B00ZIY03HS</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14652681682471787626">I'm not actually a massive fan of pulp like this. This is far past my usual books which consists of High Fantasy and Science Fiction. I did however enjoy 'The Doomsday Conspiracy' as a child by Sheldon and when I found a double book with that and this combined I figured why not.<br /><br />To start with the book is actually fairly predictable with all the intrigue, all plot devices can be seen coming a mile away, all of the hurdles are obvious in who set them up.   <span style="display:none" id="freeText14652681682471787626">I'm not actually a massive fan of pulp like this. This is far past my usual books which consists of High Fantasy and Science Fiction. I did however enjoy 'The Doomsday Conspiracy' as a child by Sheldon and when I found a double book with that and this combined I figured why not.<br /><br />To start with the book is actually fairly predictable with all the intrigue, all plot devices can be seen coming a mile away, all of the hurdles are obvious in who set them up. That doesn't mean to say there isn't a good story here. The chain pulls you along because you do want to see things work out for people. I finished at a couple hours ago and like others it left a smile on my face. <br /><br />Outside of that, I found the characters rather amusing. I could never decide whether I liked a character and my opinions on them shifted as their pasts came up and attitudes and actions effected others around them.<br /><br />It's not the most original of stories, with many a trope but past all that is a rather charming character story that will leave you smiling by the end.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15324019486085590549">I totally forgot I read this book until I was recently reminded. Shows how well the story stayed with me. What I do recall is I never did like the lead character. She never struck me as being strong despite what Mr. Sheldon was trying to accomplish. Her only weapon seemed to be her ability to fire anyone who pissed her off. Of course that meant they had to work for her first in order for her to achieve a passing appearance of power. People not on her pay roll were impervious to her cheap shots.</span>

      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1455107747">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15697961039721933706"> Wow was this a great book. Lara Cameron has had a rough life but she decides to make something of herself, becoming a real estate developer. She meets Howard Keller, who becomes her friend and mentor, and who's advice she relies on heavily, he becomes her right hand man. She also meets Paul Martin who is a great lawyer, who is much older and is married with a family but they still have an affair. She doesn't find out until later about his mafia connections. She falls in love at first sight with</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText15697961039721933706"> Wow was this a great book. Lara Cameron has had a rough life but she decides to make something of herself, becoming a real estate developer. She meets Howard Keller, who becomes her friend and mentor, and who's advice she relies on heavily, he becomes her right hand man. She also meets Paul Martin who is a great lawyer, who is much older and is married with a family but they still have an affair. She doesn't find out until later about his mafia connections. She falls in love at first sight with Philip Adler who is a brilliant pianist. Phillip and Lara get married but her business starts going downhill and someone is trying to ruin her. She has made her fair share of enemies on her way to the top. She finds out that one of the company's that isn't delivering some of her building materials for a building she must finish in time to save her company is owned by Paul Martin. In what is made to look like a mugging Philip's wrist is badly slashed so that it is useless now and he will never play the piano again. Howard reminds her that at a party that Philip wasn't at Paul said that Philip should have been by her side and needed a good talking to, she is horrified. Could Paul be behind all the bad things happening to her? <br /> The ending really shocked me so much I actually gasped, I never saw it coming. One of the best reads ever.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="15697961039721933706">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was ok">it was ok</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer911891117">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13869962551888247540">It's a story of a woman who carves out her own niche in the big bad world and makes a name for herself in one of the most male dominated professions. From there on life is full of highs and lows and how she handles it and whether she comes out of it as a winner that's to be seen. <br /><br />The story promised a strong character and the readers can be in awe of the woman and her rise from the ashes. The story line has only a few positives and very minimal surprises it springs about. It's well paced and main</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText13869962551888247540">It's a story of a woman who carves out her own niche in the big bad world and makes a name for herself in one of the most male dominated professions. From there on life is full of highs and lows and how she handles it and whether she comes out of it as a winner that's to be seen. <br /><br />The story promised a strong character and the readers can be in awe of the woman and her rise from the ashes. The story line has only a few positives and very minimal surprises it springs about. It's well paced and maintains the momentum throughout. <br /><br />The story line is not as hard hitting or gripping and the monotonous climb to success and downfall and then ifs and buts becomes too predictable. There's not much to savour in the love story too as it happens too late and leaves a little impression. An incomplete sort of end gives it a rather awkward finish. <br /><br />All in all this is not a story which will give you lots to wonder and ponder about. It leaves you high and dry in the end with everything crystal clear even before it ends. The book lacks proper direction and the fall and rise of a woman is not the saving grace for the story. <br /><br />One of the weakest books of the author. </span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="13869962551888247540">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span style="display:none" id="freeText9345334638264819842">Another amazing script by Sheldon who provides great detail of the business world involving buildings, banks, lawyers and musicians all of which give a great contribution to the planet. I must say it wasn't easy to understand how they work. Determination was described throughout making me feel so optimistic of how much can be done in life. <br /><br />On the other hand I must say the story was quite relaxing in opposite to other Sheldon's stoties who always kept me on hold from doing all other things to keep on reading. It is quite a sweet story but it's not something that causes tension or curiosity to see what's there the next page. Still enjoyed reading the book and still admire the fact how Sheldon manages to gather all kinf of information about each and every type of business, very informative.<br /><br />Will continue to gather more of his books since Sheldon is my favourite author.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked &amp;&amp; exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;name=' + shelf_name + '&amp;a=' + action + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jtNkJuu7+89T33S2Ze1aJTCUdyDAO+5dpuzuXcetZQ7rB1v1GWnvNd8HAA0bjLyXeWO0OYnmqffM5evPCziTSw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&amp;book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;refresh=true' + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('BgqmaxyyBuzsrXtMhLHEap7AWBBUYvJOTQ45VTSxsMtj3pm47mASFmB1D/f60CLY1zebCR2/teQnBzzH+CRGjg==')})
  }
//]]&gt;
</script>

    <div class=" clearFloats bigBox" id="aboutAuthor"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/9068.Sidney_Sheldon">About Sidney Sheldon</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
      <a href="/author/show/9068.Sidney_Sheldon"><img alt="9068" src="http://d.gr-assets.com/authors/1209169297p2/9068.jpg" class="right" /></a>
    <div class="readable">
      
<span id="freeTextContainer11499354901042070485">Was an American writer who won awards in three careers—a Broadway playwright, a Hollywood TV and movie screenwriter, and a best-selling novelist. His TV works spanned a 20-year period during which he created I Dream of Jeannie (1965-70), Hart to Hart (1979-84), and The Patty Duke Show (1963-66), but it was not until after he turned 50 and began writing best-selling novels such as Master of the Gam</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText11499354901042070485">Was an American writer who won awards in three careers—a Broadway playwright, a Hollywood TV and movie screenwriter, and a best-selling novelist. His TV works spanned a 20-year period during which he created I Dream of Jeannie (1965-70), Hart to Hart (1979-84), and The Patty Duke Show (1963-66), but it was not until after he turned 50 and began writing best-selling novels such as Master of the Game (1982), The Other Side of Midnight (1973) and Rage of Angels (1980) that he became most famous.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="11499354901042070485">...more</a>
